ACTOR BlueGroovyOldCoot
{
	Health 50
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Speed 3
	Scale 0.31
	PainChance 80
	Species "Enemies"	
	Monster
	SeeSound "Coot/Groovy"
	PainSound "Coot/Pain"
	DeathSound "Coot/Die"
	ActiveSound "Coot/Talk"
	Obituary "%o wasnt invited to a Groovy Old Coot's party."
	DropItem "CootAmmoDrop",64,1
	Tag "Groovy Old Coot"
	+FLOORCLIP
	+MISSILEMORE
	+MISSILEEVENMORE
	+NOINFIGHTING
	+NOBLOODDECALS
    BloodType "LeonardBlood_RR"
	Bloodcolor "ba 2c 10"
    DamageFactor "Mace", 1.1
    DamageFactor "DragonClaw", 1.5
    PainChance "MightyBoot", 255
	PainChance "MarathonStun", 255	
	var int user_scalex;
	var int user_scaley;
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		SCOO A 0
		SCOO A 1 A_JumpIfInventory("AlreadySpawned",1,"Spawn2")
		SCOO A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ReMixerSpawnScript",0,1,0)
		SCOO A 0 A_GiveInventory("AlreadySpawned",1)
	Spawn2:
		SCOO A 5 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(48,"Crouch")
		SCOO AA 2 A_Chase
		SCOO BB 2 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		SCOO CC 2 A_Chase
		SCOO DD 2 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		SCOO EE 2 A_Chase
		SCOO FF 2 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		SCOO GG 2 A_Chase
		Goto See+1 
	Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(NOPAIN,0)	
		SCOO I 10 A_FaceTarget
		SCOO H 0 A_Playsound("Leonard/PistolF")
		SCOO H 8 BRight A_CustomBulletAttack(32, 64, 1, 20, "RRPuff",0,CBAF_NORANDOM)
		SCOO I 10 A_FaceTarget
		SCOO H 0 A_Playsound("Leonard/PistolF")
		SCOO H 8 BRight
		SCOO I 8
		SCOO JKL 4 A_FaceTarget		
		Goto See
	Pain:
		SCOO Z 3 A_Pain
		SCOO ] 3 
		Goto See
	Pain.MightyBoot:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(NOPAIN,1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("duke/kickhit","body",0,0)
		SCOO Z 3 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(14)
		SCOO ] 16 A_Pain	
		Goto See
	Pain.MarathonStun:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Stop
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("NothingSpeed")
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("marathon/tech50/stun","body",0,0)
		SCOO Z 5 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_Gravity
		SCOO Z 30 A_Pain
		SCOO Z 70
		Goto See
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)		
	    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		SCOO M 5
		SCOO N 5 A_Scream
		SCOO O 5 A_NoBlocking
		SCOO P 5
		TNT1 A 0 A_playsound("redneck/thud")
		SCOO Q 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BlueGroovyOldCootCorpse", 0, 0, 0, velx, vely, velz, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_TRANSFERSCALE|SXF_ABSOLUTEVELOCITY)
		TNT1 A -1
		stop 
	XDeath:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)	
	    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid	
		RR20 A 0 A_CustomMissile("CootHead",0+Random(30,60),0+Random(35,-35),0+Random(0,370))
		RR20 A 0 A_CustomMissile("CootArm",0+Random(30,60),0+Random(35,-35),0+Random(0,370))
		RR20 A 0 A_CustomMissile("CootLeg",0+Random(30,60),0+Random(35,-35),0+Random(0,370))
		RR20 A 0 A_CustomMissile("CootLeg",0+Random(30,60),0+Random(35,-35),0+Random(0,370))  
		RR20 A 0 A_CustomMissile("MiscGib1_RR",0+Random(30,60),0+Random(35,-35),0+Random(0,370))
		RR20 A 0 A_CustomMissile("MiscGib2_RR",0+Random(30,60),0+Random(35,-35),0+Random(0,370))
		RR20 A 0 A_CustomMissile("MiscGib3_RR",0+Random(30,60),0+Random(35,-35),0+Random(0,370))
		RR20 A 0 A_CustomMissile("MiscGib4_RR",0+Random(30,60),0+Random(35,-35),0+Random(0,370))
		RR20 A 0 A_CustomMissile("MiscGib5_RR",0+Random(30,60),0+Random(35,-35),0+Random(0,370))
		RR20 A 0 A_CustomMissile("MiscGib5_RR",0+Random(30,60),0+Random(35,-35),0+Random(0,370))
		RR20 A 0 A_CustomMissile("MiscGib6_RR",0+Random(30,60),0+Random(35,-35),0+Random(0,370))	
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("Leonard/XDeath",CHAN_BODY,1.0,0,ATTN_NORM)
		ACLO E 3 A_NoBlocking
		ACLO E 8
		ACLO E -1 
		Stop	
	Crouch:

		SCOO TT 2 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)

		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BlueGroovyOldCoot_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BlueGroovyOldCoot_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BlueGroovyOldCoot_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.2*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.2*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BlueGroovyOldCoot_Shrink", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
		TNT1 A 2
		TNT1 A 0 Thing_Remove(0)
		stop
	Death.ExpanderDMG:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMG:
		SCOO A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoop
	ExpanderLoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
		loop
	ExpanderPop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		SCOO A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
	ExpanderLoopCoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
		loop
	ExpanderPopCoop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	}
}

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.0*(user_scalex/65536.0),1.0*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BlueGroovyOldCoot", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)

		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)

			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}

actor BlueGroovyOldCoot_ShrinkEffect : BlueGroovyOldCoot
{
	-ISMONSTER
	-COUNTKILL
	-SHOOTABLE
	-SOLID
	+NOINTERACTION
	-NOGRAVITY
	+CLIENTSIDEONLY	
	Renderstyle Translucent
	Alpha 0.4
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			SCOO Z 0
			SCOO Z 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			SCOO Z 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)

Actor RedGroovyOldCootCorpse
{
	Health 20
	Height 8
	Radius 16
	Mass 5000
	BloodType "LeonardBlood_RR"
	Bloodcolor "ba 2c 10"
	DamageFactor "ZorchPistol", 0.0
	DamageFactor "Zorch", 0.0
	DamageFactor "ZorchKamikaze", 0.0
	DamageFactor "PhasingZorch", 0.0
	DamageFactor "ZorchSpectral", 0.0
	+ISMONSTER
	-COUNTKILL
	-SHOOTABLE
	+VULNERABLE
	-SOLID
	+NOTARGET
	-FRIENDLY
	+NOBLOODDECALS
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			RR32 Q 4
			Loop
		Death:
			TNT1 A 0 A_RemoveMaster
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)

			TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RRGibSpawner", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			stop
		Death.RottDisintegrate:
			"####" "#" 0 A_RemoveMaster
			"####" "#" 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ExtraDeathFX",0,1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Stop
			"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("SHOOTABLE",FALSE)

			"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.9,0)
			"####" "#" 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ExtraDeathFX",0,1)
			"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.8,0)
			"####" "#" 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ExtraDeathFX",0,1)
			"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.7,0)
			"####" "#" 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ExtraDeathFX",0,1)

ACTOR GreenGroovyOldCoot : BlueGroovyOldCoot
{
	Tag "Groovy Old Coot"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		RR33 A 0
		RR33 A 1 A_JumpIfInventory("AlreadySpawned",1,"Spawn2")
		RR33 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ReMixerSpawnScript",0,1,0)
		RR33 A 0 A_GiveInventory("AlreadySpawned",1)
	Spawn2:
		RR33 A 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(48,"Crouch")
		RR33 AA 2 A_Chase
		RR33 BB 2 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		RR33 CC 2 A_Chase
		RR33 DD 2 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		RR33 EE 2 A_Chase
		RR33 FF 2 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		RR33 GG 2 A_Chase
		Goto See+1 
	Missile:
		RR33 I 10 A_FaceTarget
		RR33 H 0 A_Playsound("Leonard/PistolF")
		RR33 H 8 BRight A_CustomBulletAttack(32, 64, 1, 20, "RRPuff",0,CBAF_NORANDOM)
		RR33 I 10 A_FaceTarget
		RR33 H 0 A_Playsound("Leonard/PistolF")
		RR33 H 8 BRight
		RR33 I 8
		RR33 JKL 4 A_FaceTarget		
		Goto See

		RR33 ] 3 
		Goto See

			RR33 G 2 A_Chase("","")

			Loop
		Forget:
			"####" "#" 0 A_ClearTarget
			Goto See
		Grow:
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)

			stop
		Squish:

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)

		Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
	ExpanderLoopCoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
		loop
	ExpanderPopCoop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	}
}

ACTOR RedPantsGroovyOldCoot : BlueGroovyOldCoot
{
	Tag "Groovy Old Coot"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		RR35 A 0
		RR35 A 1 A_JumpIfInventory("AlreadySpawned",1,"Spawn2")
		RR35 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ReMixerSpawnScript",0,1,0)
		RR35 A 0 A_GiveInventory("AlreadySpawned",1)
	Spawn2:
		RR35 A 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(48,"Crouch")
		RR35 AA 2 A_Chase
		RR35 BB 2 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		RR35 CC 2 A_Chase
		RR35 DD 2 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		RR35 EE 2 A_Chase
		RR35 FF 2 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		RR35 GG 2 A_Chase
		Goto See+1 
	Missile:
		RR35 I 10 A_FaceTarget
		RR35 H 0 A_Playsound("Leonard/PistolF")
		RR35 H 8 BRight A_CustomBulletAttack(32, 64, 1, 20, "RRPuff",0,CBAF_NORANDOM)
		RR35 I 10 A_FaceTarget
		RR35 H 0 A_Playsound("Leonard/PistolF")
		RR35 H 8 BRight
		RR35 I 8
		RR35 JKL 4 A_FaceTarget		
		Goto See
	Pain:
		RR35 Z 3 A_Pain
		RR35 ] 3 
		Goto See
	Pain.MightyBoot:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(NOPAIN,1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("duke/kickhit","body",0,0)
		RR35 Z 3 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(14)
		RR35 ] 16 A_Pain
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(NOPAIN,0)		
		Goto See		
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)		
	    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		RR35 M 5
		RR35 N 5 A_Scream
		RR35 O 5 A_NoBlocking
		RR35 P 5
		TNT1 A 0 A_playsound("redneck/thud")
		RR35 Q 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RedPantsGroovyOldCootCorpse", 0, 0, 0, velx, vely, velz, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_TRANSFERSCALE|SXF_ABSOLUTEVELOCITY)
		TNT1 A -1
		stop  
	Raise:
		RR35 A 0 A_RemoveChildren(true)
		RR35 QPONM 5
		Goto See
	Death.ZorchPistol:
	Death.Zorch:

actor RedPantsGroovyOldCoot_Shrink : RedPantsGroovyOldCoot
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+COUNTKILL
	-NOGRAVITY
	+NODAMAGE
	+NOPAIN
	MaxStepHeight 0
	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 16
	Health 1
	Speed 1
	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale(scalex*0.2,scaley*0.2) // setting the scale in ACS does work, but the actor shows up at normal size for a split second
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			RR35 Z 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			RR35 A 5 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			RR35 A 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			RR35 A 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)

	Spawn2:

		Loop
	See:

		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GrayGroovyOldCoot_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GrayGroovyOldCoot_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GrayGroovyOldCoot_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.2*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.2*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GrayGroovyOldCoot_Shrink", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
		TNT1 A 2
		TNT1 A 0 Thing_Remove(0)
		stop
	Death.ExpanderDMG:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMG:
		RR36 A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoop
	ExpanderLoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
		loop
	ExpanderPop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		RR36 A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
	ExpanderLoopCoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
		loop
	ExpanderPopCoop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	}
}

			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)

		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)

			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)

Actor DarkGreenGroovyOldCootCorpse
{
	Health 20
	Height 8
	Radius 16
	Mass 5000
	BloodType "LeonardBlood_RR"
	Bloodcolor "ba 2c 10"
	DamageFactor "ZorchPistol", 0.0
	DamageFactor "Zorch", 0.0
	DamageFactor "ZorchKamikaze", 0.0
	DamageFactor "PhasingZorch", 0.0
	DamageFactor "ZorchSpectral", 0.0
	+ISMONSTER
	-COUNTKILL
	-SHOOTABLE
	+VULNERABLE
	-SOLID
	+NOTARGET
	-FRIENDLY
	+NOBLOODDECALS
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			RR37 Q 4
			Loop
		Death:
			TNT1 A 0 A_RemoveMaster
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)

			TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RRGibSpawner", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			stop
		Death.RottDisintegrate:
			"####" "#" 0 A_RemoveMaster
			"####" "#" 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ExtraDeathFX",0,1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Stop
			"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("SHOOTABLE",FALSE)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItem("RGodModeDeathSmall")
			"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.9,0)

			"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.8,0)
			"####" "#" 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ExtraDeathFX",0,1)
			"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.7,0)
			"####" "#" 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ExtraDeathFX",0,1)

			"####" "#" 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ExtraDeathFX",0,1)

			stop

ACTOR BrownGroovyOldCoot : BlueGroovyOldCoot
{
	Tag "Groovy Old Coot"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		RR38 A 0
		RR38 A 1 A_JumpIfInventory("AlreadySpawned",1,"Spawn2")
		RR38 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ReMixerSpawnScript",0,1,0)
		RR38 A 0 A_GiveInventory("AlreadySpawned",1)
	Spawn2:
		RR38 A 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(48,"Crouch")
		RR38 AA 2 A_Chase
		RR38 BB 2 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)

	Missile:

			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			RR38 G 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Samsara_Shrinker", 3) == 0, "Forget")
			Loop
		Forget:
			"####" "#" 0 A_ClearTarget
			Goto See
		Grow:
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.0*(user_scalex/65536.0),1.0*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BrownGroovyOldCoot", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 2 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 2 
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/enemygib", CHAN_BODY)
			TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeBloodPool",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}

ACTOR OrangeGroovyOldCoot : BlueGroovyOldCoot
{
	Tag "Groovy Old Coot"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		RR39 A 0
		RR39 A 1 A_JumpIfInventory("AlreadySpawned",1,"Spawn2")
		RR39 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ReMixerSpawnScript",0,1,0)
		RR39 A 0 A_GiveInventory("AlreadySpawned",1)
	Spawn2:
		RR39 A 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(48,"Crouch")
		RR39 AA 2 A_Chase
		RR39 BB 2 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)

	Missile:
		RR39 I 10 A_FaceTarget
		RR39 H 0 A_Playsound("Leonard/PistolF")
		RR39 H 8 BRight A_CustomBulletAttack(32, 64, 1, 20, "RRPuff",0,CBAF_NORANDOM)
		RR39 I 10 A_FaceTarget
		RR39 H 0 A_Playsound("Leonard/PistolF")
		RR39 H 8 BRight
		RR39 I 8
		RR39 JKL 4 A_FaceTarget		
		Goto See

		RR39 ] 3 
		Goto See

		Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
	ExpanderLoopCoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
		loop
	ExpanderPopCoop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	}
}

ACTOR GhostGroovyOldCoot : BlueGroovyOldCoot
{
	Tag "Groovy Old Coot"
	Renderstyle Translucent
	Alpha 0.5
	Painchance "ShrinkerDMG", 0
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		RR40 A 0
		RR40 A 1 A_JumpIfInventory("AlreadySpawned",1,"Spawn2")
		RR40 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ReMixerSpawnScript",0,1,0)
		RR40 A 0 A_GiveInventory("AlreadySpawned",1)
	Spawn2:
		RR40 A 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(48,"Crouch")
		RR40 AA 2 A_Chase
		RR40 BB 2 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		RR40 CC 2 A_Chase
		RR40 DD 2 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		RR40 EE 2 A_Chase
		RR40 FF 2 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		RR40 GG 2 A_Chase
		Goto See+1 
	Missile:
		RR40 I 10 A_FaceTarget
		RR40 H 0 A_Playsound("Leonard/PistolF")
		RR40 H 8 BRight A_CustomBulletAttack(32, 64, 1, 20, "RRPuff",0,CBAF_NORANDOM)
		RR40 I 10 A_FaceTarget
		RR40 H 0 A_Playsound("Leonard/PistolF")
		RR40 H 8 BRight
		RR40 I 8
		RR40 JKL 4 A_FaceTarget		
		Goto See
	Pain:
		RR40 Z 3 A_Pain
		RR40 ] 3 
		Goto See
	Pain.MightyBoot:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(NOPAIN,1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("duke/kickhit","body",0,0)
		RR40 Z 3 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(14)
		RR40 ] 16 A_Pain
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(NOPAIN,0)		
		Goto See		
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)		
	    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 7
		stop  
	Death.ZorchPistol:
	Death.Zorch:
	Death.ZorchKamikaze:
	Death.PhasingZorch:
	Death.ZorchSpectral:
		"####" "#" 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_Stop
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("DONTGIB",1)

Actor OldSkinnyCoot : BlueGroovyOldCoot
{
	Tag "Old Skinny Coot"
	SeeSound "Coot/SkinnyS"
	ActiveSound "Coot/Yell"

	States
	{
	Spawn:
		S_O2 A 0
		S_O2 A 1 A_JumpIfInventory("AlreadySpawned",1,"Spawn2")
		S_O2 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ReMixerSpawnScript",0,1,0)
		S_O2 A 0 A_GiveInventory("AlreadySpawned",1)
	Spawn2:
		S_O2 A 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(48,"Crouch")
		S_O2 AA 2 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		S_O2 BB 2 A_Chase

		S_O2 EE 2 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		S_O2 FF 2 A_Chase
		S_O2 GG 2 A_Chase("","",CHF_NOPLAYACTIVE)
		Goto See+1 
	Missile:
		S_O2 I 10 A_FaceTarget
		S_O2 H 0 A_Playsound("Leonard/PistolF")
		S_O2 H 8 BRight A_CustomBulletAttack(32, 64, 1, 20, "RRPuff",0,CBAF_NORANDOM)

		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("OldSkinnyCoot_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.2*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.2*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("OldSkinnyCoot_Shrink", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
		TNT1 A 2
		TNT1 A 0 Thing_Remove(0)
		stop
	Death.ExpanderDMG:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMG:
		S_O2 A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoop
	ExpanderLoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
		loop
	ExpanderPop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		S_O2 A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
	ExpanderLoopCoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
		loop
	ExpanderPopCoop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	}
}

{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER

	+THRUACTORS

	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 16

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.0*(user_scalex/65536.0),1.0*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("OldSkinnyCoot", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 2 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 2 
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/enemygib", CHAN_BODY)
			TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeBloodPool",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))

	}

ACTOR CootAmmoDrop : Ammo1Small
{
	Scale 0.25
	+DROPPED
	inventory.pickupmessage "Speedloader! (6 rounds of Ammo 1)"
	States
    {
      Spawn:
        RR00 A -1
        stop
	  Pickup:
        TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("MarathonClass", 0, "PickupMarathon")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("WitchavenClass", 0, "PickupWitchaven")	
  		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("RottClass", 0, "PickupRott")				
        TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("QuakeClass", 0, "PickupQuake")
        TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Clip", 6)
        stop
	  PickupRott:
	    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SMissiles", 0, "PickupFail")	  
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("SMissiles", 3)
		Stop
	  PickupWitchaven:
        TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Clip", 0, "PickupFail")
        TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Clip", 6)
        stop
      PickupMarathon:
        TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Clip", 0, "PickupFail")
        TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Clip", 6)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SetBlend("Green", 0.3, 3)
        stop
    }
}
